! Title: Search filter
! Description: ublock origin filter to remove low quality website from search engines
Expires: 7 days
google.*##.g:has(a[href*="16892.net"])
bing.*##.b_algo:has(a[href*="16892.net"])
yahoo.*##li:has(a[href*="16892.net"])
duckduckgo.*##[data-domain*="16892.net"]
searx.melashri.me##:xpath(//div[contains(@class, 'result')]/div[contains(@class, 'external-link')][contains(., '"16892.net"')]/..)]
searx.elashri.xyz##:xpath(//div[contains(@class, 'result')]/div[contains(@class, 'external-link')][contains(., '"16892.net"')]/..)]
